`tracecontext` - W3C Trace Context (default)\n  - `baggage` - W3C Baggage (default)\n  - `b3` - Zipkin B3 Single Header\n  - `b3multi` - Zipkin B3 Multi Header\n  - `jaeger` - Jaeger Uber Header\n  - `xray` - AWS X-Ray\n  - `ottrace` - OT Trace\n  - `none` - No propagation\n- Configuration example:\n  ```yaml\n  tracing:\n    enabled: true\n    propagators:\n      - tracecontext\n      - baggage\n      - b3multi\n  ```\n- Enables seamless trace correlation with services using different propagation standards\n\n### Enhanced Observability\n\n#### **Improved Trace Resource Attributes**\n- Traces now include comprehensive resource information:\n  - Service name (`flipt`)\n  - Service version\n  - Telemetry SDK details (version, language)\n  - Container information (when running in containers)\n  - Host information (hostname, OS, platform)\n  - Process runtime details (Go version, runtime name)\n- These attributes provide better context for trace filtering and analysis in observability platforms\n\n#### **OpenTelemetry Feature Flag Semantics**\n- Added support for OpenTelemetry semantic conventions for feature flags\n- Improves compatibility with observability tools that understand feature flag evaluation context\n\n## Configuration Changes\n\n### Tracing Configuration Structure\n\nThe `TracingConfig` struct now includes two new fields:\n\n```go\ntype TracingConfig struct {\n    Enabled       bool\n    Exporter      TracingExporter\n    Propagators   []TracingPropagator  // NEW\n    SamplingRatio float64              // NEW\n    Jaeger        JaegerTracingConfig\n    Zipkin        ZipkinTracingConfig\n    OTLP          OTLPTracingConfig\n}\n```\n\n### Default Configuration\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: false\n  exporter: jaeger\n  samplingRatio: 1  # Sample all traces (100%)\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext  # W3C standard\n    - baggage       # W3C baggage propagation\n  jaeger:\n    host: localhost\n    port: 6831\n  zipkin:\n    endpoint: http://localhost:9411/api/v2/spans\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\n## Deprecations\n\n**None in this release.**\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n- Fixed tracing configuration schema validation\n- Fixed tracing test compatibility with updated OTEL semconv\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### For users already using tracing:\n\n1. **No action required.** Your existing tracing configuration will work without changes.\n\n2. **Optional: Add sampling ratio configuration**\n   - If you have high-throughput environments, consider adding `samplingRatio` to reduce trace volume:\n   ```yaml\n   tracing:\n     enabled: true\n     exporter: otlp\n     samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% of traces\n   ```\n\n3. **Optional: Configure propagators**\n   - If you need to integrate traces with other services using different standards:\n   ```yaml\n   tracing:\n     enabled: true\n     propagators:\n       - tracecontext\n       - baggage\n       - b3multi  # If using Zipkin-compatible systems\n   ```\n\n### For users enabling tracing for the first time:\n\n1. **Enable tracing in your configuration:**\n   ```yaml\n   tracing:\n     enabled: true\n     exporter: otlp  # or jaeger/zipkin\n   ```\n\n2. **Configure your exporter endpoint:**\n   - For OTLP (OpenTelemetry Protocol):\n     ```yaml\n     tracing:\n       exporter: otlp\n       otlp:\n         endpoint: localhost:4317  # gRPC endpoint\n         # or\n         endpoint: http://localhost:4318  # HTTP endpoint\n         headers:\n           Authorization: \"Bearer your-token\"\n     ```\n   - For Jaeger:\n     ```yaml\n     tracing:\n       exporter: jaeger\n       jaeger:\n         host: localhost\n         port: 6831\n     ```\n   - For Zipkin:\n     ```yaml\n     tracing:\n       exporter: zipkin\n       zipkin:\n         endpoint: http://localhost:9411/api/v2/spans\n     ```\n\n3. **Optionally configure sampling and propagators:**\n   ```yaml\n   tracing:\n     enabled: true\n     exporter: otlp\n     samplingRatio: 0.1\n     propagators:\n       - tracecontext\n       - baggage\n   ```\n\n## API Changes\n\n### gRPC APIs\n\n**No breaking changes to existing gRPC services:**\n- `flipt.Flipt` service - unchanged\n- `flipt.evaluation.EvaluationService` service - unchanged\n- `flipt.evaluation.DataService` service - unchanged\n- `flipt.auth.AuthenticationService` services - unchanged\n- `flipt.analytics.AnalyticsService` service - unchanged\n- `flipt.meta.MetadataService` service - unchanged\n\n### Configuration API\n\n**No changes to configuration REST endpoints:**\n- `GET /meta/config` - unchanged\n- `GET /meta/info` - unchanged\n\n### Observability Improvements\n\nTraces from feature flag evaluation operations now include enhanced resource attributes that can be viewed in your observability platform (Jaeger, Zipkin, DataDog, Honeycomb, etc.).\n\n## Dependencies\n\n- Updated OpenTelemetry semantic conventions to latest version (v1.24.0)\n- All OTEL dependencies remain compatible with existing integrations\n\n## Known Issues\n\n**None in this release.**\n\n## Migration Path from Previous Versions\n\nThis release is fully backwards compatible. Existing configurations with tracing enabled will continue to work exactly as before.\n\n### Upgrading from v1.40.x:\n\n1. Update Flipt binary or Docker image to new version\n2.
